	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s06/06/150601963", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　あんたらが悟史くんの叔母殺しを庇わなくても！",
		   NULL, "Vous ne lui avez même pas cherché d'alibi pour le couvrir du meurtre de sa tante, mais moi, j'ai essayé, au péril de ma vie !", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s06/06/150601964", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　私は彼のアリバイのために自らを投げ打って戦った！！",
		   NULL, " Et je m'en suis sortie avec seulement trois ongles en moins,", Line_Continue);
	Wait( 3000 );
	OutputLine(NULL, "　その結果が爪３枚なんて安いもんでしょ！！",
		   NULL, " je ne les regrette pas !", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s06/06/150601965", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　でもね、それだけの努力じゃ、悟史くんを救うには……全然足りなかった…。",
		   NULL, "Sauf que même ça, ça n'a pas suffit ! Pour le sauver...", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s06/06/150601966", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "届かなかった……。",
		   NULL, "Pour le sauver, il aurait fallu beaucoup plus... Beaucoup plus.", Line_Continue);
	Wait( 1900 );
	OutputLine(NULL, "どうしてか？",
		   NULL, " Pourquoi ?", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s06/06/150601967", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　……だって、私は詩音だったんだもん。",
		   NULL, "Parce que je n'étais que Shion.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s06/06/150601968", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "…詩音は、雛見沢から遠ざけられていて、何からも外様で、何も教えられなくて、知れなくて。",
		   NULL, "Shion doit rester loin de Hinamizawa, on ne lui dit jamais rien, on fait comme si elle n'existait pas, alors elle ne peut rien savoir ! ", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s06/06/150601969", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "…でもあんたは違う。",
		   NULL, "Mais toi, c'était différent.", Line_Continue);
	Wait( 2000 );
	OutputLine(NULL, "あんたは魅音だった。",
		   NULL, " Toi, tu étais Mion.", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s06/06/150601970", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "あんたは雛見沢の内にいて、全ての中心で、全てを教えられて、全てを知ることが出来た。",
		   NULL, "Toi, tu étais à l'intérieur, au centre de tout ! Tu pouvais obtenir toutes les informations nécessaires, tu pouvais tout savoir !", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s06/06/150601971", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "私があんただったらきっと悟史くんを救えた！！",
		   NULL, "Si j'avais été toi, j'aurais pu sauver Satoshi !", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s06/06/150601972", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　私なら救ってあげられた！！！",
		   NULL, "Je l'aurais sauvé ! ", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s06/06/150601973", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　あんたが魅音になったからだ！！！",
		   NULL, "Mais je n'ai pas pu, car TU es devenue Mion !", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s06/06/150601974", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　返して魅音！！！",
		   NULL, "Rends-moi ma place de Mion !", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s06/06/150601975", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　元々魅音はあんただけのもんじゃない！",
		   NULL, "Elle n'était pas qu'à toi, au départ !", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s06/06/150601976", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　私のものでもあったはず！！！",
		   NULL, "Moi aussi, j'étais Mion, avant !", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s06/06/150601977", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　それに元々魅音は私のじゃない？！",
		   NULL, "D'ailleurs, c'était moi, Mion, avant !", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s06/06/150601978", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　私があんたに貸してあげるようになっただけで、本当は私のだったじゃないッ！！",
		   NULL, "Je t'ai juste prêté ma place, mais c'était toujours la mienne !", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s06/06/150601979", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　返せ！！",
		   NULL, "Alors rends-la-moi !", Line_Continue);
	Wait( 800 );
	OutputLine(NULL, "　私の魅音を返せッ！！！",
		   NULL, " Rends-moi mon nom ! ", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>Shion</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s06/06/150601980", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　お前が魅音の外見をしているだけでも虫唾が走る！！！",
		   NULL, "Ça me débecte, rien qu'à te voir avec mon visage, mon apparence !", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s06/06/150601981", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　お前じゃなく私が魅音だったら！",
		   NULL, " Si j'avais été Mion, comme j'aurais dû l'être, alors... Alors...", Line_Continue);
	Wait( 2000 );
	OutputLine(NULL, "　だったらぁあぁあああぁあッ！！！」",
		   NULL, " IL SERAIT VIVANT !", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();
	DrawScene("background/aka2", 1000 );

	SetSpeedOfMessage( TRUE, 128 );
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　鉄格子を蹴る、",
		   NULL, "Je frappai les barreaux de la cellule, à grands coups de pied,", Line_ContinueAfterTyping);
	PlaySE( 4, "s_down", 56, 64 );
	StartShakingOfWindow( 248, 40, 0, 2, 3*2, FALSE );
	StartShakingOfAllObjects( 248, 40, 0, 2, 3*2, TRUE );

	OutputLine(NULL, "蹴る、",
		   NULL, " de toutes mes forces,", Line_ContinueAfterTyping);
	PlaySE( 4, "s_down", 56, 64 );
	StartShakingOfWindow( 248, 40, 0, 2, 3*2, FALSE );
	StartShakingOfAllObjects( 248, 40, 0, 2, 3*2, TRUE );

	OutputLine(NULL, "蹴る。",
		   NULL, " encore et encore.", Line_ContinueAfterTyping);
	PlaySE( 4, "s_down", 56, 64 );
	StartShakingOfWindow( 248, 40, 0, 2, 3*2, FALSE );
	StartShakingOfAllObjects( 248, 40, 0, 2, 3*2, TRUE );
	OutputLineAll(NULL, "", Line_Normal);

	ClearMessage();

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "　魅音はまるで、鉄格子が蹴り倒されてその下敷になるのを避けるかのように、",
		   NULL, "À chaque coup que je portai aux barreaux, Mion recula, terrorisée,", Line_WaitForInput);
	OutputLine(NULL, "…奥で、鉄格子を蹴る音に怯えて縮こまるだけだった。",
		   NULL, " comme si j'allais pouvoir l'écraser avec, et elle se terra en glapissant contre la paroi du fond, poussant des cris de peur à chaque nouveau coup...", Line_Normal);
	SetSpeedOfMessage( FALSE, 0 );
	ClearMessage();

	CallScript( "&eyeCamp" );
	FadeOutBGM( 0, 1000, TRUE );
	SetValidityOfSkipping( FALSE );
	DrawSceneWithMask("tips/gettip_meak020", "mask1900", 7, 0, 400 );
	Wait( 5000 );
	DrawSceneWithMask("black", "mask1900", 7, 0, 400 );
	SetValidityOfSkipping( TRUE );
}
